posted:Posted January 27, 2024
msg:Taiyuan R&F Wanda Hotel reviews
1) Public areas (lobby, elevator, restaurant, floor corridor): In the climate of minus 13 degrees Celsius, no heating and air conditioning are turned on at all. You must wear a thick down jacket and a hat.

2) Western restaurant on the first floor:
   a) Checking in on Saturday night, I happily went straight to the Western restaurant and had a buffet meal at a star hotel to start the vacation mode. Result: freezing to death. The first bite of the meal we took was still warm, and the second bite was already cold... We were not given a chance to comment on whether the food was delicious, because the restaurant was too cold and the food went cold.
   b) The daily breakfast was also spent in this way. The breakfast may be really good, but I really didn‚Äôt have the chance to get to know it because the whole environment was too cold. It‚Äôs really not an exaggeration. I wore a thick down jacket and a hat to eat breakfast. of. I really couldn't eat anything. The only hot food I could eat was hot soy milk and freshly made noodles. Under such circumstances, the hot soy milk often ran out; before taking the porridge, remember to test the temperature. In order to keep warm, I filled a large bowl of millet porridge, but it turned out to be ice... yes, it was ice.
   c) Plate/porcelain spoon: It is cold when picked up. Star hotels should ensure that all utensils are heated. This is unqualified.

3) Guest room:
   a) Room 808: The bathroom makes a deep, uninterrupted sound, similar to a "man's breath". Oh my god, I thought I was staying in a **. The hotel engineering team came to inspect and said that the toilet was leaking water, causing the sound in the pipes. At 11 o'clock in the evening, we asked the front desk to change our room. Fortunately, the front desk was very helpful and allowed us to change rooms without saying a word.
   c) After changing rooms, everything became normal. It was clean. The room service was still very good, and the heating and hot water in the room were sufficient.
   d) There is no iron or iron stand for ironing clothes in the guest room.
   e) There is no ordering service in the guest room. I searched for a long time but couldn't find the room service menu. Every time I come back tired after a long day out, I want to stay in the hotel to dine. The restaurant was so cold that the only option was room service - which didn't work either.

Overall, this is our first time visiting Taiyuan, Shanxi. We are InterContinental Hotel members and want a change of taste, so Wanda is the place to stay. The result is very disappointing. It is already 2024. I feel that this hotel is a star hotel from 30 years ago and cannot keep up with the pace of the world.

Taiyuan, after all, is the capital city of Shanxi Province. Five-star hotels in the provincial capital city should work harder to improve soft services. In the winter, in order to save money, I am reluctant to turn on the air conditioning in the public areas. If the guest experience is not good, I will not come back.

Shanxi has a profound cultural heritage, and we love the indoor and outdoor museums everywhere. Next Friday we will come to Taiyuan to visit the museum, but we will no longer stay at Wanda. I will never stay at Wanda again when I go to other cities in the future. It is really a fake five-star hotel.

I rolled down the car window and asked him why he didn‚Äôt let me in. He replied that there was no room. At this time, a car came out of the exit. I asked again if I could enter. I asked him the exact location of the parking lot, and impatiently told me to just go ahead. Then we continued to move forward. Unexpectedly, there was no entrance to the parking lot. The entrance is Wanda Plaza, and it was during the evening rush hour, so it was very congested. 2. When checking in, I specifically asked the closing time of the swimming pool at the front desk, and was told that it was 11 o'clock in the evening. After seeing it, many parents hurriedly let their children go ashore.
3. The obsolete facilities and equipment are understandable, but the hygienic situation is really unreasonable, and it can be described as dirty. The corners of the room are full of dust that has not been cleaned for many years, the faucet is full of water stains, and there is no detailed cleaning at all. The floor in the elevator is sticky. The most intolerable thing is the locker room in the fitness center, which is not as good as an ordinary bathing center.
4. I don‚Äôt know how other rooms are. The shower room in the room I live in still has potential safety hazards. The actual switch direction of hot and cold water is opposite to that marked.
The above situation was also reported to the lobby manager during the stay, and I hope it will change in the future.
I would like to thank Ctrip for its coordination and assistance throughout the process.
